(_( AG_NNP ._. )_)
Imperial_NNP Dairy_NNP Institute_NNP ,_, Bangalore_NNP (_( Received_VBN for_IN publication_NN on_IN 17th_CD November_NNP 1937_CD )_) No_DT study_NN has_VBZ so_RB far_RB been_VBN made_VBN of_IN the_DT composition_NN of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN buffaloes_NNS ,_, and_CC the_DT analysis_NN of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN the_DT Indian_JJ dairy_NN cow_NN has_VBZ been_VBN made_VBN only_RB in_IN the_DT Montgomery_NNP breed_NN ,_, by_IN Shah_NNP [_NNP 1936_CD ]_NNP ._.
In_IN this_DT experiment_NN a_DT more_JJR detailed_JJ analysis_NN of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN cows_NNS and_CC buffaloes_NNS ,_, than_IN has_VBZ hitherto_VBN been_VBN done_VBN by_IN any_DT previous_JJ worker_NN ,_, has_VBZ been_VBN carried_VBN out_RP with_IN a_DT view_NN to_TO make_VB a_DT comparative_JJ study_NN of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN these_DT two_CD types_NNS of_IN dairy_NN animals_NNS ._.
The_DT most_RBS striking_JJ difference_NN between_IN normal_JJ milk_NN and_CC colostrum_NN is_VBZ in_IN the_DT amount_NN of_IN globulin_NN ,_, a_DT protein_NN that_WDT occurs_VBZ in_IN blood_NN and_CC in_IN traces_NNS only_RB in_IN ordinary_JJ milk_NN ,_, but_CC is_VBZ present_JJ in_IN colostrum_NN in_IN a_DT comparatively_RB large_JJ amount_NN ._.

The_DT animals_NNS selected_VBN for_IN the_DT investigation_NN were_VBD from_IN the_DT two_CD important_JJ Indian_JJ dairy_NN breeds_NNS maintained_VBD at_IN the_DT Imperial_NNP Dairy_NNP Institute_NNP Farm_NNP ,_, Banga-_NNP lore_NN ,_, viz._NN ,_, three_CD Sindhi_NNP cows_NNS and_CC three_CD Murrah_NNP buffaloes_NNS ._.

ANALYTICAL_NNP METHODS_NNP The_DT determination_NN of_IN the_DT proteins_NNS was_VBD carried_VBN out_RP by_IN the_DT newer_JJR methods_NNS of_IN protein_NN analysis_NN suggested_VBN by_IN Moir_NNP ,_, and_CC adopted_VBN by_IN Bergman_NNP and_CC Turner_NNP [_NNP 1937_CD ]_NN in_IN their_PRP$ analysis_NN of_IN goats_NNS '_POS colostrum_NN ._.
(_( 29_CD )_) 30_CD Colostrum_NNP of_IN the_DT Dairy_NNP Cow_NNP and_CC the_DT Dairy_NNP Buffalo_NNP The_DT total_JJ protein_NN was_VBD precipitated_VBN by_IN warm_JJ trichloracetic_JJ acid_NN ,_, thereby_RB leaving_VBG the_DT non-protein_JJ nitrogen_NN in_IN solution_NN ._.

Casein_NNP and_CC globulin_NN were_VBD precipitated_VBN together_RB by_IN the_DT addition_NN of_IN a_DT saturated_JJ solution_NN of_IN magnesium_NN sulphate_NN ,_, after_IN first_JJ neutralising_VBG the_DT sample_NN to_TO phenolphthalein_VB with_IN sodium_JJ hydroxide_NN ._.

After_IN the_DT precipitation_NN was_VBD complete_JJ ,_, the_DT solution_NN was_VBD filtered_VBN in_IN a_DT pressure_NN filter_NN and_CC the_DT residue_NN was_VBD washed_VBN with_IN a_DT saturated_JJ salt_NN solution_NN ._.
The_DT nitrogen_NN content_NN was_VBD determined_VBN as_IN for_IN total_JJ protein_NN ._.
The_DT amount_NN of_IN albumin_NN was_VBD calculated_VBN by_IN subtracting_VBG casein_NN and_CC globulin_NN from_IN total_JJ protein_NN ,_, while_IN the_DT difference_NN between_IN casein_NN and_CC globulin_NN and_CC casein_NN gave_VBD the_DT globulin_NN content_NN of_IN the_DT sample_NN ._.
The_DT specific_JJ gravity_NN was_VBD determined_VBN by_IN the_DT Westphal_NNP balance_NN at_IN a_DT tem-_JJ perature_NN of_IN 20°C_CD ._.

TABLE_NN I_PRP Composition_NNP of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN Murrah_NNP buffaloes_NNS V._NNP SIVASUBRAMANIAN_NNP AND_NNP C._NNP W._NNP DOVER_NNP 31_CD TABLE_NNP II_NNP Composition_NNP of_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN Sindhi_NNP cows_VBZ 32_CD Colostrum_NNP of_IN the_DT Dairy_NNP Cow_NNP and_CC the_DT Dairy_NNP Buffalo_NNP The_DT high_JJ percentage_NN of_IN total_JJ protein_NN in_IN the_DT earliest_JJS stages_NNS of_IN the_DT colostral_JJ period_NN is_VBZ due_JJ mainly_RB to_TO the_DT high_JJ globulin_NN content_NN ._.
Buffaloes_NNP '_POS colostrum_NN shows_VBZ a_DT higher_JJR content_NN of_IN total_JJ protein_NN than_IN cows_NNS '_POS colostrum_NN ,_, and_CC in_IN both_DT cases_NNS there_EX is_VBZ a_DT fall_NN which_WDT is_VBZ more_RBR rapid_JJ during_IN the_DT first_JJ twenty-four_JJ hours_NNS after_IN parturition_NN than_IN the_DT following_JJ days_NNS ._.
Both_DT casein_NN and_CC albumin_NN behave_VBP similarly_RB in_IN that_DT they_PRP are_VBP present_JJ in_IN large_JJ amounts_NNS at_IN the_DT time_NN of_IN calving_NN ,_, and_CC subsequently_RB show_VB a_DT gradual_JJ fall_NN ._.
In_IN these_DT constituents_NNS ,_, also_RB buffaloes_VBZ '_POS colostrum_NN is_VBZ richer_JJR than_IN cows_NNS '_POS colostrum_NN ._.
The_DT important_JJ part_NN which_WDT globulin_NN plays_NNS in_IN the_DT transmission_NN of_IN anti-_JJ bodies_NNS from_IN the_DT mother_NN to_TO her_PRP$ young_JJ justifies_NNS the_DT separate_JJ analysis_NN of_IN this_DT protein_NN ,_, which_WDT has_VBZ not_RB so_RB far_RB been_VBN done_VBN in_IN previous_JJ investigations_NNS on_IN the_DT colostrum_NN of_IN bovines_NNS ._.
Starting_VBG at_IN the_DT high_JJ figure_NN of_IN 10.9_CD per_IN cent_NN in_IN buffaloes_NNS and_CC 6.2_CD per_IN cent_NN in_IN cows_NNS ,_, it_PRP falls_VBZ abruptly_RB within_IN the_DT first_JJ twenty-four_JJ hours_NNS by_IN about_IN 75_CD per_IN cent_NN in_IN the_DT former_JJ and_CC 50_CD per_IN cent_NN in_IN the_DT latter_NN ._.
The_DT rapidity_NN of_IN the_DT subsequent_JJ fall_NN ,_, though_RB not_RB as_RB great_JJ as_IN in_IN the_DT beginning_NN ,_, is_VBZ sufficient_JJ to_TO result_VB in_IN only_JJ traces_NNS of_IN this_DT protein_NN fraction_NN being_VBG left_VBN in_IN the_DT normal_JJ milk_NN ._.
SUMMARY_NNP 1_CD ._.
Buffaloes_NNP '_POS colostrum_NN is_VBZ higher_JJR in_IN specific_JJ gravity_NN ,_, acidity_NN ,_, sodium_NN chloride_NN ,_, total_JJ solids_NNS ,_, total_JJ protein_NN ,_, casein_NN ,_, albumin_NN ,_, globulin_NN and_CC ash_NN than_IN cows_NNS '_POS colostrum_NN ,_, while_IN in_IN lactose_JJ it_PRP is_VBZ lower_JJR ._.
2_CD ._.
In_IN both_DT animals_NNS there_EX is_VBZ a_DT progressive_JJ fall_NN in_IN all_PDT the_DT constituents_NNS except_IN lactose_NN which_WDT shows_VBZ an_DT increase_NN and_CC fat_JJ which_WDT is_VBZ irregular_JJ ._.
3_CD ._.
Globulin_NNP constitutes_VBZ the_DT major_JJ part_NN of_IN the_DT total_JJ protein_NN of_IN both_DT kinds_NNS of_IN colostrum_NN soon_RB after_IN calving_VBG ,_, and_CC its_PRP$ decrease_NN is_VBZ more_RBR marked_JJ during_IN the_DT first_JJ twenty-four_JJ hours_NNS after_IN parturition_NN than_IN during_IN the_DT remainder_NN of_IN the_DT colostral_JJ period_NN ._.
4_CD ._.
Buffaloes_NNP '_POS colostrum_NN changes_NNS to_TO normal_JJ milk_NN in_IN about_IN three_CD days_NNS ,_, while_IN cows_NNS '_POS colostrum_NN takes_VBZ about_IN four_CD days_NNS ._.

of_IN blood_NN was_VBD used_VBN daily_RB by_IN the_DT worms_NNS ._.
This_DT is_VBZ the_DT minimal_JJ figure_NN and_CC probably_RB the_DT actual_JJ amount_NN would_MD be_VB several_JJ times_NNS more_RBR ._.

Lungworms_NNS are_VBP specially_RB dangerous_JJ in_IN calves_NNS ,_, sheep_NN and_CC goats_NNS ._.
Another_DT worm_NN which_WDT is_VBZ particularly_RB dangerous_JJ to_TO young_JJ animals_NNS is_VBZ the_DT ascarid_JJ parasite_NN of_IN calves_NNS and_CC foals_NNS ._.
Though_NNP ,_, in_IN the_DT adult_NN stage_NN ,_, amphis-_JJ tomes_NNS are_VBP practically_RB harmless_JJ ,_, they_PRP are_VBP highly_RB pathogenic_JJ in_IN their_PRP$ immature_NN stages_NNS which_WDT are_VBP passed_VBN in_IN the_DT duodenum_NN and_CC intestine_NN ._.

Datta_NNP [_NN 1933_CD ]_NN has_VBZ recorded_VBN the_DT finding_NN of_IN ``_`` Actinomycosis_NNP ``_`` in_IN a_DT buffalo-heifer_NN in_IN growths_JJ ``_`` on_IN the_DT parotid_JJ glands_NNS of_IN both_DT sides_NNS ``_`` ._.
The_DT specimen_NNS referred_VBD to_TO by_IN him_PRP has_VBZ been_VBN studied_VBN further_RBR by_IN the_DT author_NN and_CC its_PRP$ description_NN will_MD appear_VB later_RB (_( p._VB 278_CD )_) ._.

(_( 395_CD )_) 396_CD Aspergillus_NNP from_IN a_DT case_NN of_IN Skin_NNP Disease_NNP in_IN a_DT Dog_NNP CULTURAL_NNP CHARACTERS_NNP The_DT material_NN was_VBD cultured_VBN with_IN some_DT difficulty_NN in_IN plain_NN agar_NN ._.
